! HARMONIC FUNCTIONS

! --------------------------------------------------------------



! Constants

TQGCAL:=1.997E-3; ! TQ gradient calibration per amp in T m-1 A-1, divide by B-rho for k

!HQ are not normalised to momentum 

HQCAL:=1.25; ! Scaling factor for HQ for HQ=1 (multiply by value -10 -> +10 for D7cos etc)

brho:=1.23; !injection value - change for later



! Values as input on control system

D7SIN=0.0;

D7COS=0.0;

D8SIN=0.0;

D8COS=0.0;

F8SIN=0.0;

F8COS=0.0;

! Useful for future

F9SIN=0.0;

F9COS=0.0;



! Amplitudes and Harmonics for QTD

da1:=D7COS*HQCAL*TQGCAL/brho;

db1:=D7SIN*HQCAL*TQGCAL/brho;

dhn1:=7;



da2:=D8COS*HQCAL*TQGCAL/brho;

db2:=D8SIN*HQCAL*TQGCAL/brho;

dhn2:=8;



! Amplitude and Harmonic for QTF

fa1:=F8COS*HQCAL*TQGCAL/brho;

fb1:=F8SIN*HQCAL*TQGCAL/brho;

fhn1:=8;



fa2:=F9COS*HQCAL*TQGCAL/brho; !doesn't exist in control system, but useful for future/models

fb2:=F9SIN*HQCAL*TQGCAL/brho;

fhn2:=9;



HER0qtd:=(da1*cos(dhn1*(0/10)*2*PI))+(db1*sin(dhn1*(0/10)*2*PI))+(da2*cos(dhn2*(0/10)*2*PI))+(db2*sin(dhn2*(0/10)*2*PI));

HER1qtd:=(da1*cos(dhn1*(1/10)*2*PI))+(db1*sin(dhn1*(1/10)*2*PI))+(da2*cos(dhn2*(1/10)*2*PI))+(db2*sin(dhn2*(1/10)*2*PI));

HER2qtd:=(da1*cos(dhn1*(2/10)*2*PI))+(db1*sin(dhn1*(2/10)*2*PI))+(da2*cos(dhn2*(2/10)*2*PI))+(db2*sin(dhn2*(2/10)*2*PI));

HER3qtd:=(da1*cos(dhn1*(3/10)*2*PI))+(db1*sin(dhn1*(3/10)*2*PI))+(da2*cos(dhn2*(3/10)*2*PI))+(db2*sin(dhn2*(3/10)*2*PI));

HER4qtd:=(da1*cos(dhn1*(4/10)*2*PI))+(db1*sin(dhn1*(4/10)*2*PI))+(da2*cos(dhn2*(4/10)*2*PI))+(db2*sin(dhn2*(4/10)*2*PI));

HER5qtd:=(da1*cos(dhn1*(5/10)*2*PI))+(db1*sin(dhn1*(5/10)*2*PI))+(da2*cos(dhn2*(5/10)*2*PI))+(db2*sin(dhn2*(5/10)*2*PI));

HER7qtd:=(da1*cos(dhn1*(7/10)*2*PI))+(db1*sin(dhn1*(7/10)*2*PI))+(da2*cos(dhn2*(7/10)*2*PI))+(db2*sin(dhn2*(7/10)*2*PI));

HER8qtd:=(da1*cos(dhn1*(8/10)*2*PI))+(db1*sin(dhn1*(8/10)*2*PI))+(da2*cos(dhn2*(8/10)*2*PI))+(db2*sin(dhn2*(8/10)*2*PI));

HER9qtd:=(da1*cos(dhn1*(9/10)*2*PI))+(db1*sin(dhn1*(9/10)*2*PI))+(da2*cos(dhn2*(9/10)*2*PI))+(db2*sin(dhn2*(9/10)*2*PI));



HER0qtf:=(fa1*cos(fhn1*(0/10)*2*PI))+(fb1*sin(fhn1*(0/10)*2*PI))+(fa2*cos(fhn2*(0/10)*2*PI))+(fb2*sin(fhn2*(0/10)*2*PI));
